***госпитализировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:госпитализировать.html>госпитализи́ровать</a> (18254)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">hospitalisieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to hospitalize</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:госпиталь.html>го́спиталь</a> (2347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">hospital</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">hôpital</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпиталь.html>го́спиталь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">góspitalʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпиталь.html>го́спиталя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпиталь.html>го́спитали</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпиталь.html>го́спиталей</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпиталь.html>госпитале́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hospital
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тыловой.html>тылово́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:госпиталь.html>го́спиталь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tylovój <b>góspitalʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">base <b>hospital</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:господин.html>господи́н</a> (537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:господь.html>госпо́дь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Gospódʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:господин.html>господи́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gospodín</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:господин.html>господи́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:господин.html>господа́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:господин.html>госпо́д</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпожа.html>госпожа́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gentleman <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a man of a higher rank or position</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>mister <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an address to any male, especially if his name or proper address is unknown</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>Mr.</li>
<li>lord; master</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:господний.html>госпо́дний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gospódnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>God's, Lord's
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:господний.html>госпо́дни</a></b> неисповеди́мы</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">putí <b>gospódni</b> neispovedímy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">God works in mysterious ways</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">срань <b><a href = vnd.unilang:господний.html>госпо́дняя</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sranʹ <b>gospódnjaja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">holy shit!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:господствовать.html>госпо́дствовать</a> (14621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:господствовать.html>госпо́дствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gospódstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to rule, to reign</li>
<li>to predominate, to prevail</li>
<li>to command, to dominate, to tower above</li></ol>

***госпожа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:госпожа.html>госпожа́</a> (4167)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gospoďa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпожа.html>госпожа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gospožá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпожа.html>госпожи́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпожа.html>госпожи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:госпожа.html>госпо́ж</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:господин.html>господи́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dame, lady <i>(a woman of a higher rank or position)</i></li>
<li>madam, ma'am</li>
<li>Mrs. or Miss + name</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гостеприимный.html>гостеприи́мный</a> (9636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***гость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>гость</a> (489)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gostь</i>,  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰóstis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>гость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>го́стя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>го́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>госте́й</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гостья.html>го́стья</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>guest, visitor
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>го́сти</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí v <b>gósti</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go visiting</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>гостя́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ v <b>gostjáx</b> u kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be a guest of someone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> merchant, especially one that trades overseas.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>Гость</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Gostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> may refer to a guest of either gender, but is always a masculine noun; any adjectives modifying it must be masculine, as must any pronouns referring back to it.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гостевой.html>гостево́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gostevój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:государев.html>госуда́рев</a> (12931)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государь.html>госуда́рь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gosudárʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ев</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ev</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gosudárstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государственный.html>госуда́рственный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gosudárstvennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)госуда́рственнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)госуда́рственней</b>)
</p>

<li>national</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> public
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:государственный.html>госуда́рственный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:переворот.html>переворо́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gosudárstvennyj</b> perevorót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">coup d'état</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">public revolution</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рство</a> (502)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государь.html>госуда́рь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gosudárʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sovereign</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gosudárstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">government</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> State
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пока.html>пока́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рство</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́ды</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:государство.html>госуда́рства</a></b>. (влади́мир ле́нин)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Poká jestʹ <b>gosudárstvo</b>, net svobódy. Kogdá búdet svobóda, ne búdet <b>gosudárstva</b>. (Vladímir Lénin)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">While the State exists, there can be no freedom. When there is freedom there will be no State. (Vladimir Lenin)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***государь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:государь.html>госуда́рь</a> (2578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:государь.html>госуда́рь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gosudarĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a later form of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">господарь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gospodarĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> The reshaping of the latter has been explained by the influence of the root <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">суд-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sud-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to judge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> or by a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/relaxed_pronunciation" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:relaxed pronunciation">relaxed pronunciation</a><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***готический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:готический.html>готи́ческий</a> (16390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гот.html>гот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">got</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***готовить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:готовить.html>гото́вить</a> (1546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовый.html>гото́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gotóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовить.html>гото́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gotóvitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовить.html>пригото́вить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подготовить.html>подгото́вить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заготовить.html>загото́вить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to prepare, to make ready
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовить.html>пригото́вить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prigotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cook
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовить.html>пригото́вить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prigotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to prepare, to train
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подготовить.html>подгото́вить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podgotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to store up, to lay in <i>(stock)</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заготовить.html>загото́вить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zagotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:готовиться.html>гото́виться</a> (1559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовить.html>гото́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовиться.html>гото́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gotóvitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подготовиться.html>подгото́виться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовиться.html>пригото́виться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get ready, to prepare <i>oneself</i>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приготовиться.html>пригото́виться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prigotóvitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to study, to prepare for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:готовиться.html>гото́вятся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мену</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní <b>gotóvjatsja</b> k ekzámenu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they are studying for the exam</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подготовиться.html>подгото́виться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podgotóvitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be impending, to be imminent, to be threatening</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовить.html>гото́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gotóvitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годовой.html>годово́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доклад.html>докла́д</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:готовиться.html>гото́вится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:реальный.html>реа́льной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:информация.html>информа́ции</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Godovój doklád <b>gotóvitsja</b> na osnóve reálʹnoj informácii.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The annual report is prepared based on real information.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ol><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> предл. <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> + <a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́т</a>. п.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приготовление.html>приготовле́ния</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:приводить.html>приводи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:состояние.html>состоя́ние</a> приспособленности <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожидаемый.html>ожида́емому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тию</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>Кома́нда</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упорно.html>упо́рно</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовиться.html>гото́вится</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответственный.html>отве́тственному</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступление.html>выступле́нию</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><a href = vnd.unilang:ожидать.html>ожида́ть</a> какого-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тия</a> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурный.html>Бу́рные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обсуждение.html>обсужде́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сеть.html>сеть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стукач.html>стукаче́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорый.html>ско́ро</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:достигнуть.html>дости́гли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>уше́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:администрация.html>администра́ции</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:почувствовать.html>почу́вствовала</a>: что-то <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:готовиться.html>гото́вится</a></span>! </span></li>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еда.html>еде́</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:создаваться.html>создава́ться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:приготовляться.html>приготовля́ться</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
